\hypertarget{filtering-the-tables}{%
\subsubsection{Filtering the tables}\label{filtering-the-tables}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# filtering TREE table}
\NormalTok{tree_tab <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{AL_TREE}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{TREE}
\NormalTok{tree_tab <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(tree_tab,}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(CN, PLT_CN, PREV_TRE_CN, INVYR, COUNTYCD, PLOT, SUBP, CONDID, STATUSCD, SPCD, DIA, HT, SPGRPCD,CR, CCLCD,SPGRPCD,UNITCD))}
\NormalTok{tree_tab <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tree_tab }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{diam =}\NormalTok{ (}\FloatTok{2.54} \OperatorTok{*}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tree_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{DIA ))}
\NormalTok{tree_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tree_tab }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\OperatorTok{-}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(DIA))}
\NormalTok{tree_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{DIA<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tree_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{diam}
\NormalTok{tree_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{tree_tab }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\OperatorTok{-}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(diam))}
 
\CommentTok{# filtering PLOT table}
\NormalTok{plot_tab <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{AL_PLOT}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{PLOT}
\NormalTok{plot_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(plot_tab, }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(PLOT, INVYR, COUNTYCD, LAT, LON, ELEV, RDDISTCD, ECOSUBCD))}
\NormalTok{plot_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(plot_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTYCD,plot_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{PLOT, }\DataTypeTok{sep=}\StringTok{"_"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{plot_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{plot_tab }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{filter}\NormalTok{(INVYR}\OperatorTok{>=}\DecValTok{2009}\NormalTok{)}
 
\CommentTok{# filtering COND table}
\NormalTok{cond_tab <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{AL_COND}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COND}
\NormalTok{cond_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(cond_tab, }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(CN, PLT_CN, INVYR, COUNTYCD, PLOT, FORTYPCD, STDAGE, STDORGCD, DSTRBCD1,TRTCD1, SITECLCD, SICOND,PHYSCLCD, FIRE_SRS, GRAZING_SRS, OWNCD, STAND_STRUCTURE_SRS, BALIVE,SISP,SLOPE,ASPECT))}
\NormalTok{cond_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cond_tab }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{filter}\NormalTok{(INVYR}\OperatorTok{>=}\DecValTok{2009}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{cond_tab<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{cond_tab }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTYCD) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(PLOT, }\DataTypeTok{.by_group=}\OtherTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{cond_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(cond_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTYCD,cond_tab}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{PLOT, }\DataTypeTok{sep=}\StringTok{"_"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{biomass-equation}{%
\subsection{Biomass equation}\label{biomass-equation}}

\hypertarget{logbiomassb0b1logdia--biomass-expbo-b1logdia}{%
\paragraph{\texorpdfstring{log(biomass)=B0+B1\emph{log(DIA)----\textgreater{}
biomass= exp(BO+
B1}log(DIA))}{log(biomass)=B0+B1log(DIA)----\textgreater{} biomass= exp(BO+ B1log(DIA))}}\label{logbiomassb0b1logdia--biomass-expbo-b1logdia}}

\_0 and \_1 are determined using species' taxonomic identity and wood
specific gravity (green volume to dry-weight basis) (Chojnacky, Heath,
and Jenkins 2014; Miles and Smith 2009).

\hypertarget{calculating-species-richness-s-and-shannon-weiners-diversity-index-h}{%
\subsection{calculating species richness (S) and shannon-weiner's

(H)}\label{calculating-species-richness-s-and-shannon-weiners-diversity-index-h}}

species richness

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{compdata_AL<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{compdata_AL }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{S =} \KeywordTok{n_distinct}\NormalTok{(SPCD)) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Shannon-Weiner's diversity index

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CNTY_PLT_SUB_SPCD<-}\KeywordTok{paste}\NormalTok{(compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT_SUB,compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{SPCD,}\DataTypeTok{sep=}\StringTok{"#"}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{#lets compute shannon's index}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{compdata_AL }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB,SPCD,S,bio_change))}
\CommentTok{#total individuals}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{totind =} \KeywordTok{n}\NormalTok{()) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}
\CommentTok{#number of each species}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB, SPCD) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{indsp =} \KeywordTok{n}\NormalTok{()) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}
\CommentTok{#ratio}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{p =}\NormalTok{ indsp}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{totind)}
\CommentTok{#pln(p)}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{plnp =}\NormalTok{ p}\OperatorTok{*}\KeywordTok{log}\NormalTok{(p))}
\CommentTok{#sum1}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB,SPCD) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{sum1 =} \KeywordTok{mean}\NormalTok{(plnp))}\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}
\CommentTok{#final sum}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{summ=} \KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(sum1)) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}
\CommentTok{#final step}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{H=} \DecValTok{-1}\OperatorTok{*}\NormalTok{summ)}
\NormalTok{compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{H <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{H[}\KeywordTok{match}\NormalTok{(compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT_SUB,shdata}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT_SUB)]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{we-also-looked-at-using-basal-area-to-calculate-h-but-decided-against-using-it-here-is-the-code-for-that-calculation-anyways}{%
\paragraph{we also looked at using basal area to calculate H but decided
against using it, here is the code for that calculation
anyways}\label{we-also-looked-at-using-basal-area-to-calculate-h-but-decided-against-using-it-here-is-the-code-for-that-calculation-anyways}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# making proportions based on BA }
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{compdata_AL }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB,SPCD,CNTY_PLT_SUB_SPCD,BA))}
\CommentTok{#species within plot BA}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(CNTY_PLT_SUB_SPCD) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{spsum=} \KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(BA))}
\CommentTok{#totalplot BA}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB) }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{pltsum =} \KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(BA))}
\CommentTok{#proportion}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{p=}\NormalTok{ spsum}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{pltsum)}
\NormalTok{compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{prop <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{p[}\KeywordTok{match}\NormalTok{(compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CNTY_PLT_SUB_SPCD,shdata}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{CNTY_PLT_SUB_SPCD)]}

\CommentTok{#now applying Shannons using that proportion}
\CommentTok{#pln(p)}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{plnp =}\NormalTok{ p}\OperatorTok{*}\KeywordTok{log}\NormalTok{(p))}
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\OperatorTok{!}\KeywordTok{duplicated}\NormalTok{(CNTY_PLT_SUB_SPCD)) }
\NormalTok{shdata<-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{group_by}\NormalTok{(COUNTY_PLOT_SUB)}\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{H=}\OperatorTok{-}\DecValTok{1}\OperatorTok{*}\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(plnp))}

\NormalTok{compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{HBA <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{shdata}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{H[}\KeywordTok{match}\NormalTok{(compdata_AL}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT_SUB, shdata}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{COUNTY_PLOT_SUB)]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

now to remove duplicated lines and negative biomass change

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
